While Parquet focuses on efficient storage on disk 
and fast retrieval, Arrow focuses on fast in memory 
execution and data exchange. ^Lhp9LM6z

In a row-oriented storage, the data is laid out one row at a time ^Dmxc98my

In a column-oriented storage, it is laid out one column at a time ^jilNKSwF
